
=== Zvfbfa - Additional BF16 vector compute support extension

[[policy-variant-vector-single-width-bfloat-add-subtract]]
==== Vector Single-Width BFloat Add/Subtract Intrinsics

[[policy-variant-narrowing-float-to-bfloat-type-convert]]
==== Narrowing Float to BFloat Type-Convert Intrinsics

[,c]
----
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vfncvt_f_f_w_bf16mf4_tu(vbfloat16mf4_t vd,
                                               vfloat32mf2_t vs2, size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vfncvt_rod_f_f_w_bf16mf4_tu(vbfloat16mf4_t vd,
                                                   vfloat32mf2_t vs2,
                                                   size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf2_t __riscv_vfncvt_f_f_w_bf16mf2_tu(vbfloat16mf2_t vd,
                                               vfloat32m1_t vs2, size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf2_t __riscv_vfncvt_rod_f_f_w_bf16mf2_tu(vbfloat16mf2_t vd,
                                                   vfloat32m1_t vs2, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfncvt_f_f_w_bf16m1_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vfloat32m2_t vs2,
                                             size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfncvt_rod_f_f_w_bf16m1_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd,
                                                 vfloat32m2_t vs2, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m2_t __riscv_vfncvt_f_f_w_bf16m2_tu(vbfloat16m2_t vd, vfloat32m4_t vs2,
                                             size_t vl);
vbfloat16m2_t __riscv_vfncvt_rod_f_f_w_bf16m2_tu(vbfloat16m2_t vd,
                                                 vfloat32m4_t vs2, size_t vl);
